6HPLVWUXFWXUHG LQWHUYLHZV
Interview guide  
Topic 
Hybrid power plants, consisting of solar, wind, and batteries (energy storage) have a future in renewable 
electricity grids where flexibility is highly valued. They have the capability to more closely mimic conventional 
power plants, while using 100% renewable energy sources. This thesis is trying to answer the question of what the 
value of including planning restrictions and social impacts in the modelling of hybrid power plants during the pre-
feasibility study is. We are trying to understand how companies currently go through the planning process for 
hybrid power plants, with particular interest in the pre-feasibility phase.  
# 
Question 
Priority 
Opening questions 
1.  
What is your role within the company? 
1 
2.  
How many development projects of hybrid power plants have been involved with? 
2 
Process overview 
3.  
What are the major milestones for a hybrid power plant project prior to the final investment 
decision?  
4 
4.  
What is done to decrease the level of unknowns for a hybrid power plant development project 
during this part of the project? 
4 
Pre-feasibility and feasibility study  
5.  
How do you evaluate the economic/technical feasibility of the plant? 
5 
a. 
What assumptions go into the evaluation? 
3 
b. 
How do you think this evaluation could be improved? 
4 
c. 
How would/do you evaluate the value of improving the evaluation? 
5 
6.  
What is the most essential economical, technical, and regulatory data needed to deliver 
satisfactory estimates in the pre-feasibility phase?  
5 
a. 
How do you mitigate inaccurate key assumptions? 
E.g. the CAPEX cost of a piece of equipment is inaccurate or a regulatory piece of information 
was missed or misinterpreted? 
3 
7.  
How do you budget during the pre-feasibility phase?  
E.g. are you already accounting for the economic impact from getting approval from locals  
5 
a. 
How much capital are you typically allocating to dealing with social issues? 
E.g. 2-5% of total CAPEX? 
5 
Social 
8.  
How can you predict the level of resistance towards a project within a local community? 
5 
a. 
How much does CAPEX increase based on the level of resistance a project is facing? 
5 
9.  
How can a project end up being cancelled excluding financial and regulatory reasons? 
E.g. what needs to happen in the local community for a project to become unappealing or 
blocked entirely? 
5 
a. 
How do you avoid that such eventualities occur? 
5 
b. 
How do you account for the risk of such occurrences?  
4 
10.  
What tools/activities do you do to deal with social acceptance in the local community? 
4 
a. 
When do you start using these tools? 
3 
11.  
How do you judge which activities/tools will help gain the most social acceptance in the local 
community? 
4 
Planning 
12.  
When do you start considering planning restrictions? 
4 
13.  
How do you take planning restrictions into account? 
4 
14.  
How do/would you include planning restrictions in the technical/economic evaluation of the 
plant? 
5 
15.  
How are delays in construction-start date and commercial operation date handled? 
4 
Warm down / ending section 
16.  
What part of the current planning process works well, and which parts could be improved 
inside your company? 
3 
17.  
Are there any changes to your current process that you are working on or would like to 
implement?  
4 
18.  
What do you think the future will look like for hybrid power plants?  
2
